Microsoft.EntityFrameworkCore.Database.Command: Information: Executed DbCommand (4ms) [Parameters=[], CommandType='Text', CommandTimeout='30']
SELECT [r].[RolID], [r].[DescripcionRol], [r].[NombreRol], [t].[RolID], [t].[PermisoID], [t].[PermisoID0], [t].[DescripcionPermiso], [t].[Modulo], [t].[NombrePermiso]
FROM [Roles] AS [r]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [r0].[RolID], [r0].[PermisoID], [p].[PermisoID] AS [PermisoID0], [p].[DescripcionPermiso], [p].[Modulo], [p].[NombrePermiso]
    FROM [RolPermisos] AS [r0]
    INNER JOIN [Permisos] AS [p] ON [r0].[PermisoID] = [p].[PermisoID]
) AS [t] ON [r].[RolID] = [t].[RolID]
ORDER BY [r].[RolID], [t].[RolID], [t].[PermisoID]

Microsoft.EntityFrameworkCore.Database.Command: Information: Executed DbCommand (1ms) [Parameters=[], CommandType='Text', CommandTimeout='30']
SELECT [r].[RolID], [r].[DescripcionRol], [r].[NombreRol], [t].[RolID], [t].[PermisoID], [t].[PermisoID0], [t].[DescripcionPermiso], [t].[Modulo], [t].[NombrePermiso]
FROM [Roles] AS [r]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [r0].[RolID], [r0].[PermisoID], [p].[PermisoID] AS [PermisoID0], [p].[DescripcionPermiso], [p].[Modulo], [p].[NombrePermiso]
    FROM [RolPermisos] AS [r0]
    INNER JOIN [Permisos] AS [p] ON [r0].[PermisoID] = [p].[PermisoID]
) AS [t] ON [r].[RolID] = [t].[RolID]
ORDER BY [r].[RolID], [t].[RolID], [t].[PermisoID]

FROM (
    SELECT TOP(1) [r].[RolID], [r].[DescripcionRol], [r].[NombreRol]
    FROM [Roles] AS [r]
    WHERE [r].[RolID] = @__id_0
) AS [t]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [r0].[RolID], [r0].[PermisoID], [p].[PermisoID] AS [PermisoID0], [p].[DescripcionPermiso], [p].[Modulo], [p].[NombrePermiso]
    FROM [RolPermisos] AS [r0]
    INNER JOIN [Permisos] AS [p] ON [r0].[PermisoID] = [p].[PermisoID]
) AS [t0] ON [t].[RolID] = [t0].[RolID]
ORDER BY [t].[RolID], [t0].[RolID], [t0].[PermisoID]

SELECT [r].[RolID], [r].[DescripcionRol], [r].[NombreRol], [t].[RolID], [t].[PermisoID], [t].[PermisoID0], [t].[DescripcionPermiso], [t].[Modulo], [t].[NombrePermiso]
FROM [Roles] AS [r]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [r0].[RolID], [r0].[PermisoID], [p].[PermisoID] AS [PermisoID0], [p].[DescripcionPermiso], [p].[Modulo], [p].[NombrePermiso]
    FROM [RolPermisos] AS [r0]
    INNER JOIN [Permisos] AS [p] ON [r0].[PermisoID] = [p].[PermisoID]
) AS [t] ON [r].[RolID] = [t].[RolID]
ORDER BY [r].[RolID], [t].[RolID], [t].[PermisoID]
